 Let us tell you such tips that will easily make work pressure handle 1
 aap jaanate he ki kal aapkaa senior nahin aane vaala to iskaa matlab ye he ki kaam kaa sara boj aapke najuk kandhon par hoga
 In such a situation, you should understand the working pattern of them
